 He said, "foreign lawyers have already made meaningful inroads into India's legal domain with the 'come and go' policy (temporarily come and go) and technology will further develop it
 pratispardhaa kaa saamana karnaa bhartiya vakeelon ke liye bhi laabhadaayak hoga

" '' wilkins ne kaha ki videshi vakeelon ko bhartiya adaalaton ke samaksh upasthit hone par bahut kam phayda hoga or jo pesh honge unhen bhi sabit karnaa hoga ki unhen bhartiya kanoon or prakriya kii paryaapt jaankaree he
 In important cases before the Supreme Court of India, hardly any foreign or domestic petitioner should appoint any foreign lawyer in front of experienced lawyers Fali Nariman, Harish Salve, Kapil Sibal, Gopal Subrahmanyam and Abhishek Manu Singhvi
 '' The law professor further said that Indian lawyers will eventually learn more from their foreign counterparts by opening the Indian law market
 vahiin bhartiya vakeelon ko desh main hi rahane par adhik protsaahan milegaa

 In Raipur, the bungalow of Renuka Singh, BJP leader and former woman child development minister in Chhattisgarh, has been taken over by the Andhra Bank
 renuka singh par 13 lakh 86 hajaar 638 rupee andhra bank kaa lone bakaayaa tha
 Renuka Singh and his son Yashwant Singh have been named in the capture notice issued from the Raipur branch of Andhra Bank as the person who took the loan
 bank ne baqayada ishtehaar jari kar kabza notice kii soochna jari kii he
 The property is Bangla HIG 83 located in Purana area
 bank ke mutabik purv mantri renuka singh ne raipur kii VIP road par 4032 foot plot par makaan banane ke liye bank se 20 lakh rupee kaa karj liya tha, lekin samay par kisht kii adaayagi nahin kii
 The bank gave Renuka Singh time till 22 December 2017 to repay the loan
 nirdhaarit tithi par bakaayaa bhugtan nahin hone kii vajah se bank ne unke bangale ko apane kabje main le liya
 In the commercials issued by the bank, the former minister has been warned not to behave in relation to the confiscated assets of the bank
 udhar bank kii karrwai se tilamilaai renuka singh kaa daawa he ki ve aath lakh kii rakam jamaa kar chuki hai
 However, due to some reasons the balance could not be accumulated
 unke mutabik wo lone chukaana chaahati hai, lekin is tarah se ishtehaar jari kar bank ne unhen apamaanit kiya he
 Former minister Renuka Singh is known as the bjp's female leader in Ambikapur division
 ve do baar prem nagar vidhaan sabha seat se bijepi kii vidhayak rah chuki hai
 In his second term, Chief Minister Raman Singh entrusted him with the responsibility of Minister of Women and Child Development
 haalanki varsh 2013 ke vidhaan sabha chunaav main ve prem nagar vidhaan sabha seat se congressi ummidavaar se 18 hajaar maton se haar gayi thi

 yah pehla mauka he jab bijepi ke kisi kaddavar netaa ko bank ne karj kii adaayagi ko lekar aaina dikhaaya he

 mana ja rahaa he ki isi kadi main purv mantri renuka singh ke karj kaa maamla bhi surkiyon main aa gaya
